(The art of using pigments to ornament fabricks has an ancient origin.  The discovery of fragment of a madder - dyed fabric at Mohenjo - daro sticking to a silver vase, would led us to believe that the mardent proses of dyeing cloth was known in India five thousand years ago)  Indian Printed Textiles.  Page. 4.  Published by All-India Handicrafts Board, Ministry of Commerce & Industry Government of India.
